0.9.1037
- [Perf] Prompt Workbench major performance improvement: Side Panel preview content now skips rendering during Layout events; Body reduced from ~8ms to ~0.3ms (97% reduction).
- [Perf] Workbench converted from popup window to inline rendering (matching RimTalk architecture), eliminating dual-window GUI context overhead.
- [Perf] Module list rows simplified to ButtonText (4→1 Widget per row), redundant metadata row removed.
- [Perf] Preview renderer Layout guard added, font pre-rasterization.
- [Cleanup] Removed UGUI dead code (~850 lines, 10 files), removed debug performance diagnostics.
- [Version] About/About.xml modVersion bumped to 0.9.1037.

0.9.1036
- [Fix] Social circle and strategy generation perspective attribution bug: player's first-person statements were incorrectly attributed to faction leaders in social news posts (e.g., player says "I don't need your iron", NPC's faction publishes it as their own statement).
  * TryAnalyzeDialogueKeywords now analyzes only AI text (NPC response) instead of merged player+AI text — social news is published from the NPC's perspective; including player text polluted keyword/sentiment classification.
  * TryGenerateRandomDialogueSocialPost no longer passes player's raw message as intentHint to TryBuildFactionDialoguePublicClaim, preventing "{Faction} says: {player's words}" misattribution.
  * Category/sentiment inference in the same method now uses AI text only instead of merged text.

0.9.1035
- [Optimization] Dramatically reduced GameComponent per-tick performance overhead (4-round architectural refactor):
  * GameComponent_NpcDialoguePushManager: Dictionary/HashSet O(1) indexes for factionPushStates/queues/windows; eliminated LINQ Where/OrderBy/ToList per-tick allocations; globalDeliveryTicks min-value caching.
  * GameComponent_RPGManager: Full pawn sweep replaced with multi-frame scan (1 map per tick), peak from 4.38ms to microsecond level; scan interval increased from 900 to 9000 ticks; ultra-light early-return after bootstrap completes; persona target caching; pending check O(1) HashSet.
  * GameComponent_DiplomacyManager (god component split):
    - SocialCircle subsystem extracted to GameComponent_SocialCircleManager, removed from DiplomacyManager per-tick path.
    - DelayedEvents + EventQueries extracted to GameComponent_DelayedEventManager, event processing reduced from every 60 to every 250 ticks.
    - RPGManager restored to independent GameComponentTick (ultra-light early return), no longer routed through DiplomacyManager.
    - Presence evaluation added per-faction hourly cache, eliminating repeated Rand.PushState/PopState.
    - ProcessPeriodicDiplomacySnapshots fully async (LongEventHandler), main thread only updates indices.
    - SnapshotCache.Tick reduced from every tick to every 60 ticks.
    - ProcessDelayedEvents HashSet allocation eliminated (reverse RemoveAt).
    - HandleInboundFactionMessage double ForcePresenceOnline eliminated.
    - RefreshPresenceOnDialogueOpen unreachable dead code removed.
  * SocialCircleState: ProcessedOrigins, FactionActionCooldowns, PublishedPostOriginKeys all O(1) Dictionary/HashSet indexes.
  * Multiple hot-path optimizations: Initialize methods de-LINQ'd, ResolveMentionedFaction ToLowerInvariant deduplication, EnqueueDeferredSocialNewsSeed O(1), GetLastNegotiatorForSession reverse index loop.
- [Version] About/About.xml modVersion bumped to 0.9.1035.

0.9.1034
- [Fix] AI-ended diplomacy conversations were permanently blocked from re-initiation. ExitDialogue/GoOffline/SetDnd now recover via cooldown: ExitDialogue auto-reconnects after 2 hours; GoOffline/SetDnd auto-clear ended state when presence recovers to Online. Legacy saves recover instantly on load.
- [Tweak] ExitDialogue diplomacy cooldown extended from 1 to 2 in-game hours.
- [New] Fuzzy cooldown hint "They need a moment... (available within ~X hours)" shown during cooldown instead of hard block text.

0.9.1029
- [Fix] When airdrop quantity is clamped by system limits, payment is now proportionally scaled: when validatedCount < requestedOriginalCount, DeductionPlan is scaled down to actual needed cost (item + shipping), eliminating the "overpay with no refund" cause of full deduction with partial delivery.
- [Fix] Removed artificial stack cap from candidate window: ComputeMaxDeliverableByStacks no longer participates in hardMax clamping; BuildStacks auto-expands stack count to accommodate full quantity.
- [Fix] Removed the 5000 hardcoded quantity cap in airdrop offers; now only validates positive numbers.
- [Fix] Airdrop arrival notification total price now uses the settled shipping cost from the confirmed trade snapshot instead of recalculating at delivery time.
- [Guard] Added delivery quantity invariance guard, preventing full deduction with partial delivery.
- [Docs] Synced `doc/VersionLog.txt` and `doc/VersionLog_en.txt`.

0.9.1023
- `/models` fallback + raw passthrough on structured-parse failure + strict JSON preamble (root fix across validation and dialogue paths):
  1. [Diagnostics] `ApiUsabilityDiagnosticService.RunCloudDiagnosticCoroutine` now treats only `404/405/501` as “models endpoint missing”; in this case it skips strict model-availability gating and promotes `chat probe + contract` to final availability truth.
  2. [Diagnostics] Cloud usability test now succeeds (with warning detail) when `/models` is missing but chat is reachable; non-missing failures (`429/5xx/network`) remain fail-fast.
  3. [Local diagnostics] `ProbeLocalServiceCoroutine` no longer marks OpenAI-compatible local service as down when `/v1/models` returns `404/405/501`; it proceeds to chat probe for final validation.
  4. [Dialogue path] `AIChatServiceAsync.ProcessRequestCoroutine` removes fixed immersion fallback sentence after structured-envelope retries are exhausted, and switches to raw model text passthrough with explicit logging tag.
  5. [Prompting] Added a strict JSON format preamble (`### Format Requirement` equivalent + `visible_dialogue` JSON example) at the beginning of response-contract sections for both RPG and diplomacy, visible in workbench preview.

0.9.1019
- Ransom window anchoring and social-news compatibility fix (systemic execution-chain update):
  1. [Social news compatibility] `BuildUnifiedChannelSystemPrompt` no longer fail-fast aborts on `social_circle_post` native render compatibility mismatch; it now logs a warning and continues with structured fallback prompt text.
  2. [Stable single-target reference] `FactionDialogueSession` now stores single-target ransom snapshot (`target/current_ask/min/max`) and builds `[RansomOfferReference]`; `BuildAiUserMessage` injects it every turn, independent of history compression retention.
  3. [Single-target pre-execution clamp] `TryHandlePrisonerRansomActionWithSelection` now clamps out-of-range `offer_silver` to the nearest snapshot boundary before execution and logs normalization details.
  4. [Batch total auto-rewrite] `BuildBatchRansomExecutionPlan` now normalizes out-of-window batch totals by clamping total to nearest boundary, proportional per-target rescale, fractional-residual integer distribution, and exact-sum rewrite; mathematically infeasible boundaries still fail-fast.
  5. [Prompt contract conflict cleanup] Removed legacy "offer_silver has no upper/lower limit" wording and unified contract semantics to "reference system window + pre-execution normalization" across `SystemPromptConfig`, default prompt template, and `action_rules.txt`.

0.9.1017
- Vehicle Pawn crash root fix (RimTalk Persona vs RPG eligibility decoupling):
  1. [Root Fix] `PawnDialogueRoutingPolicy.IsRpgDialogueEligibleRace` now uses a capability-aware whitelist: Humanlike/Mechanoid/Animal remain RPG-dialogue eligible; ToolUser must have both `story+skills`, which blocks VehiclePawn/shell Pawn types from entering RPG eligibility.
  2. [New] Added `IsRimTalkPersonaSyncEligible`: applies an extra persona-subsystem gate on top of RPG eligibility, and explicitly excludes Animal from RimTalk Persona sync (Animal keeps RPG dialogue only).
  3. [Block] Added fail-fast guards in `TrySyncPawnPersonaFromRimTalkSafely` and `IsEligibleRimTalkPersonaCopyTarget`; ineligible pawns are skipped before any RimTalk `GetPersonality(Pawn)` reflection call.
  4. [Cleanup] `CleanupInvalidRpgDictionaries` now removes persisted persona entries for pawns that can be resolved but no longer satisfy RPG eligibility (including vehicle-like pawns), while preserving old-save compatibility.
  5. [Consistency] `ShouldUseRpgDialogue` now validates target pawn eligibility; `GetIneligibleRaceReason` now aligns with the same eligibility rules so menu visibility and executable routing stay consistent.

0.9.1015
- Prompt workbench performance optimization Plan A (lightweight caching optimization):
  1. [Opt] Token fragment caching: PromptWorkbenchChipEditor added _cachedTokenFragments cache, only recalculates token positions when text/rect/style changes, eliminating per-frame TryBuildTokenFragments calls (expensive text layout calculations);
  2. [Opt] Preview build frame skipping: RimChatSettings_PromptSectionWorkspace added PromptWorkspacePreviewFrameSkip=2, checks preview build every 3 frames (from 60fps to 20fps), reducing 66% preview build CPU usage;
  3. [Opt] Content height caching: EnhancedTextArea added _cachedContentHeight cache, only recalculates height when text/width/style changes, reducing GC allocations.

0.9.1014
- Prompt workbench UI rendering pipeline deep performance optimization (eliminated ~200 per-frame heap allocations):
  1. [Opt] BuildModules result caching: added GetCachedPromptWorkspaceModules method, returns cached module list when channel and layouts unchanged, eliminating per-frame BuildModules + LINQ sorting + GetOrderedMainChainSections;
  2. [Opt] Eliminated redundant Clone in Layout caches: GetPromptWorkspaceNodeLayouts/SectionLayouts/EditableNodes return cached list directly on cache hit (write paths ensured safe via cache invalidation), eliminating ~50+ Clone + 6 new List per frame;
  3. [Opt] GetOrderedMainChainSections caching: added layout-content-signature-based cache, avoiding per-frame creation of 2 Dictionary + 1 List + sorting;
  4. [Opt] Color static-ization: extracted ~30 new Color() calls into static readonly fields, eliminating per-frame construction overhead;
  5. [Fix] Removed duplicate HandlePromptWorkspaceKeyboardShortcuts call in DrawPromptWorkspaceEditorPanel.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1014.

- Prompt immersion and format optimization: 7-module fix (immersion first, token saving second):

  4. [P1] FOV information filtering: Added IsPawnPrivyToColonyInfo check — when the other party in dialogue is not a player faction member (prisoner/hostile/foreign), suppresses colony inventory and alert data to prevent omniscient information leakage;
  5. [P2] action_rules format instruction deduplication: Removed redundant format constraints duplicated with api_limits/quest_guidance/response_contract, condensed to one minimization principle + commitment-action binding rule;

  5. [New] MovePromptSectionLayout/DrawSectionLayoutRowButtons methods, Section sort logic consistent with Node sort;
  6. [Refactor] PromptWorkbenchModuleProjection.BuildModules now accepts sectionLayouts parameter, Section order driven by persisted data;
  7. [Refactor] Prompt build pipeline fully integrated with Section custom ordering: PromptSectionAggregateBuilder, WorkspacePreviewIncremental, WorkbenchComposer, SectionAggregates;
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1011.

0.9.1015
- Prompt workbench performance optimization Plan A (lightweight caching optimization):
  1. [Opt] Token fragment caching: PromptWorkbenchChipEditor added _cachedTokenFragments cache, only recalculates token positions when text/rect/style changes, eliminating per-frame TryBuildTokenFragments calls (expensive text layout calculations);
  2. [Opt] Preview build frame skipping: RimChatSettings_PromptSectionWorkspace added PromptWorkspacePreviewFrameSkip=2, checks preview build every 3 frames (from 60fps to 20fps), reducing 66% preview build CPU usage;
  3. [Opt] Content height caching: EnhancedTextArea added _cachedContentHeight cache, only recalculates height when text/width/style changes, reducing GC allocations.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1015.

0.9.1014
- Prompt workbench UI rendering pipeline deep performance optimization (eliminated ~200 per-frame heap allocations):
  1. [Opt] BuildModules result caching: added GetCachedPromptWorkspaceModules method, returns cached module list when channel and layouts unchanged, eliminating per-frame BuildModules + LINQ sorting + GetOrderedMainChainSections;
  2. [Opt] Eliminated redundant Clone in Layout caches: GetPromptWorkspaceNodeLayouts/SectionLayouts/EditableNodes return cached list directly on cache hit (write paths ensured safe via cache invalidation), eliminating ~50+ Clone + 6 new List per frame;
  3. [Opt] GetOrderedMainChainSections caching: added layout-content-signature-based cache, avoiding per-frame creation of 2 Dictionary + 1 List + sorting;
  4. [Opt] Color static-ization: extracted ~30 new Color() calls into static readonly fields, eliminating per-frame construction overhead;
  5. [Fix] Removed duplicate HandlePromptWorkspaceKeyboardShortcuts call in DrawPromptWorkspaceEditorPanel.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1014.

0.9.1013
- Prompt workbench preview rendering performance optimization (frame rate recovered from ~80fps to ~800fps):
  1. [Opt] Subsection layout caching: added SubsectionLayoutEntry list cache, moving per-frame CalcHeight calls into EnsureLayoutCache, eliminating per-frame height calculations;
  2. [Opt] SectionLayout list caching: added _promptWorkspaceSectionLayoutCacheChannel cache in RimChatSettings_PromptSectionWorkspace.NodeLayout.cs, avoiding per-frame list cloning;
  3. [Opt] ComposeValues caching: added CachedComposeValues dictionary to incremental preview build state in PromptWorkspacePreviewModels.cs, ensuring BuildDeterministicComposeValues called only once per build session;
  4. [Opt] GUIStyle caching: replaced new GUIStyle() calls with instance field caches, eliminating per-frame GC allocations;
  5. [Fix] CS0162 warning: fixed loop logic error in DrawSubsectionBody.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1013.

0.9.1008
- Root fix: AI ignores its own observable state (e.g., eating but claiming nothing is in front of it), dialogue inertia overrides system-injected facts — systemic fix:
  1. Added [Self-Action Consistency] section to rpg_state_anchor: declares Recent Job State and Needs data as true observable state with priority above prior dialogue self-descriptions; when dialogue history contradicts data, prior output is wrong and must be acknowledged and corrected;
  2. Expanded rpg_state_anchor [Contradiction Self-Correction] from faction-only to all system-injected facts (faction relations, settlement power, self observable state);
  3. Added anchor contradiction example "eating but claiming nothing is in front of you", explicitly listing self-action denial from dialogue inertia as roleplay failure;
  4. UnifiedCatalogMigrationTargetVersion 6→7, added ApplyRpgStateAnchorSelfActionMigration one-time migration (covers any/rpg/proactive_rpg channels);
  5. Synchronized PromptUnifiedDefaults.cs C# fallback and PromptUnifiedCatalog_Default.json JSON defaults.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1008.

0.9.1009
- Prompt immersion and format optimization: 7-module fix (immersion first, token saving second):
  1. [P0] Hediff-Need state fusion: Added ResolveHediffLabelWithContext method — when a Hediff label (e.g., "Malnutrition") contradicts a recovered Need (e.g., Food >40%), appends context annotation (e.g., "eating") to prevent LLM hallucination on stale Hediff labels;
  2. [P0] Protocol violation retry message history leak: Added IsProtocolViolationMessage filter in ConvertFromChatMessages, blocking DIALOGUE_PROTOCOL_VIOLATION/RPG_CONTRACT_VIOLATION/TEXT_INTEGRITY_VIOLATION/IMMERSION_VIOLATION prefixed retry messages from compressed persistent history, preventing format instruction leakage in subsequent dialogue turns;
  3. [P1] Action Space conditional pruning: Added ApplyActionExclusions method, auto-excluding inapplicable actions based on DialogueScenarioContext social identity signals — non-prisoner NPCs exclude ReduceResistance/ReduceWill/Recruit, non-player faction leaders exclude RomanceAttempt/MarriageProposal/Date;
  4. [P1] FOV information filtering: Added IsPawnPrivyToColonyInfo check — when the other party in dialogue is not a player faction member (prisoner/hostile/foreign), suppresses colony inventory and alert data to prevent omniscient information leakage;
  5. [P2] action_rules format instruction deduplication: Removed redundant format constraints duplicated with api_limits/quest_guidance/response_contract, condensed to one minimization principle + commitment-action binding rule;
  6. [P2] rpg_state_anchor compression: Compressed from ~800 to ~400 chars, retaining core constraints (power perception/behavior consistency/contradiction self-correction), removing redundant examples;
  7. [P2] thought_chain streamlining: Compressed from 16 thought items to 8 core items, removing detail constraint items duplicated with repetition_reinforcement; added TurnCount to RpgPromptTurnContextRuntime for future tiered rendering;
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1015
- Prompt workbench performance optimization Plan A (lightweight caching optimization):
  1. [Opt] Token fragment caching: PromptWorkbenchChipEditor added _cachedTokenFragments cache, only recalculates token positions when text/rect/style changes, eliminating per-frame TryBuildTokenFragments calls (expensive text layout calculations);
  2. [Opt] Preview build frame skipping: RimChatSettings_PromptSectionWorkspace added PromptWorkspacePreviewFrameSkip=2, checks preview build every 3 frames (from 60fps to 20fps), reducing 66% preview build CPU usage;
  3. [Opt] Content height caching: EnhancedTextArea added _cachedContentHeight cache, only recalculates height when text/width/style changes, reducing GC allocations.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1015.

0.9.1014
- Prompt workbench UI rendering pipeline deep performance optimization (eliminated ~200 per-frame heap allocations):
  1. [Opt] BuildModules result caching: added GetCachedPromptWorkspaceModules method, returns cached module list when channel and layouts unchanged, eliminating per-frame BuildModules + LINQ sorting + GetOrderedMainChainSections;
  2. [Opt] Eliminated redundant Clone in Layout caches: GetPromptWorkspaceNodeLayouts/SectionLayouts/EditableNodes return cached list directly on cache hit (write paths ensured safe via cache invalidation), eliminating ~50+ Clone + 6 new List per frame;
  3. [Opt] GetOrderedMainChainSections caching: added layout-content-signature-based cache, avoiding per-frame creation of 2 Dictionary + 1 List + sorting;
  4. [Opt] Color static-ization: extracted ~30 new Color() calls into static readonly fields, eliminating per-frame construction overhead;
  5. [Fix] Removed duplicate HandlePromptWorkspaceKeyboardShortcuts call in DrawPromptWorkspaceEditorPanel.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1014.

0.9.1013
- Prompt workbench preview rendering performance optimization (frame rate recovered from ~80fps to ~800fps):
  1. [Opt] Subsection layout caching: added SubsectionLayoutEntry list cache, moving per-frame CalcHeight calls into EnsureLayoutCache, eliminating per-frame height calculations;
  2. [Opt] SectionLayout list caching: added _promptWorkspaceSectionLayoutCacheChannel cache in RimChatSettings_PromptSectionWorkspace.NodeLayout.cs, avoiding per-frame list cloning;
  3. [Opt] ComposeValues caching: added CachedComposeValues dictionary to incremental preview build state in PromptWorkspacePreviewModels.cs, ensuring BuildDeterministicComposeValues called only once per build session;
  4. [Opt] GUIStyle caching: replaced new GUIStyle() calls with instance field caches, eliminating per-frame GC allocations;
  5. [Fix] CS0162 warning: fixed loop logic error in DrawSubsectionBody.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1013.

0.9.1012
- Prompt workbench UI high-fidelity alignment with RimTalk and preview optimization:
  1. [Fix] Clicking "Prompt Workbench" Tab now directly opens the large popup (Dialog_PromptWorkbenchLarge), removing the Launcher intermediate page;
  2. [Refactor] Module list aligned with RimTalk entry UI: Section now has enable/disable checkbox, unified row height 25f, bottom bar ▲▼ sort buttons replace inline buttons;
  3. [New] PromptSectionLayoutConfig now has Enabled field, supporting Section-level enable/disable control;
  4. [Refactor] Module list sorted by Slot+Order (Section+Node interleaved), matching preview assembly order (WYSIWYG);
  5. [New] Single entry preview: when Section/Node is selected, side panel shows only that entry's content; added "Full Preview" Tab toggle;
  6. [Refactor] Editor toolbar aligned with RimTalk: module label + enable toggle + Slot selector + order display;
  7. [Opt] Preview performance: frame budget increased from 0.002s to 0.008s, full preview build frozen while editor has focus;
  8. [New] PromptWorkbenchInfoPanel.FullPreview enum, side panel has 3 tabs: Preview | Full Preview | Variables;
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1012.

0.9.1011
- Prompt workbench large window restored and Section free-order sorting:
  1. [Fix] Restored OpenPromptWorkbenchWindow to open large-size popup (Dialog_PromptWorkbenchLarge), mistakenly deprecated in previous version;
  2. [New] Added PromptSectionLayoutConfig persistence model, supporting Section order state serialization (Scribe_Collections);
  3. [New] PromptSectionSchemaCatalog.GetOrderedMainChainSections method, returns sections ordered by persisted layout data;
  4. [New] Added ▲▼ sort buttons to Section items in DrawPromptWorkspaceModuleList, unified with Node sort operations;
  5. [New] MovePromptSectionLayout/DrawSectionLayoutRowButtons methods, Section sort logic consistent with Node sort;
  6. [Refactor] PromptWorkbenchModuleProjection.BuildModules now accepts sectionLayouts parameter, Section order driven by persisted data;
  7. [Refactor] Prompt build pipeline fully integrated with Section custom ordering: PromptSectionAggregateBuilder, WorkspacePreviewIncremental, WorkbenchComposer, SectionAggregates;
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1011.

0.9.1009
- Prompt immersion and format optimization: 7-module fix (immersion first, token saving second):
  1. [P0] Hediff-Need state fusion: Added ResolveHediffLabelWithContext method — when a Hediff label (e.g., "Malnutrition") contradicts a recovered Need (e.g., Food >40%), appends context annotation (e.g., "eating") to prevent LLM hallucination on stale Hediff labels;
  2. [P0] Protocol violation retry message history leak: Added IsProtocolViolationMessage filter in ConvertFromChatMessages, blocking DIALOGUE_PROTOCOL_VIOLATION/RPG_CONTRACT_VIOLATION/TEXT_INTEGRITY_VIOLATION/IMMERSION_VIOLATION prefixed retry messages from compressed persistent history, preventing format instruction leakage in subsequent dialogue turns;
  3. [P1] Action Space conditional pruning: Added ApplyActionExclusions method, auto-excluding inapplicable actions based on DialogueScenarioContext social identity signals — non-prisoner NPCs exclude ReduceResistance/ReduceWill/Recruit, non-player faction leaders exclude RomanceAttempt/MarriageProposal/Date;
  4. [P1] FOV information filtering: Added IsPawnPrivyToColonyInfo check — when the other party in dialogue is not a player faction member (prisoner/hostile/foreign), suppresses colony inventory and alert data to prevent omniscient information leakage;
  5. [P2] action_rules format instruction deduplication: Removed redundant format constraints duplicated with api_limits/quest_guidance/response_contract, condensed to one minimization principle + commitment-action binding rule;
  6. [P2] rpg_state_anchor compression: Compressed from ~800 to ~400 chars, retaining core constraints (power perception/behavior consistency/contradiction self-correction), removing redundant examples;
  7. [P2] thought_chain streamlining: Compressed from 16 thought items to 8 core items, removing detail constraint items duplicated with repetition_reinforcement; added TurnCount to RpgPromptTurnContextRuntime for future tiered rendering;
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1015
- Prompt workbench performance optimization Plan A (lightweight caching optimization):
  1. [Opt] Token fragment caching: PromptWorkbenchChipEditor added _cachedTokenFragments cache, only recalculates token positions when text/rect/style changes, eliminating per-frame TryBuildTokenFragments calls (expensive text layout calculations);
  2. [Opt] Preview build frame skipping: RimChatSettings_PromptSectionWorkspace added PromptWorkspacePreviewFrameSkip=2, checks preview build every 3 frames (from 60fps to 20fps), reducing 66% preview build CPU usage;
  3. [Opt] Content height caching: EnhancedTextArea added _cachedContentHeight cache, only recalculates height when text/width/style changes, reducing GC allocations.

0.9.1009.

0.9.1008
- Root fix: AI ignores its own observable state (e.g., eating but claiming nothing is in front of it), dialogue inertia overrides system-injected facts — systemic fix:
  1. Added [Self-Action Consistency] section to rpg_state_anchor: declares Recent Job State and Needs data as true observable state with priority above prior dialogue self-descriptions; when dialogue history contradicts data, prior output is wrong and must be acknowledged and corrected;
  2. Expanded rpg_state_anchor [Contradiction Self-Correction] from faction-only to all system-injected facts (faction relations, settlement power, self observable state);
  3. Added anchor contradiction example "eating but claiming nothing is in front of you", explicitly listing self-action denial from dialogue inertia as roleplay failure;
  4. UnifiedCatalogMigrationTargetVersion 6→7, added ApplyRpgStateAnchorSelfActionMigration one-time migration (covers any/rpg/proactive_rpg channels);
  5. Synchronized PromptUnifiedDefaults.cs C# fallback and PromptUnifiedCatalog_Default.json JSON defaults.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1008.

0.9.1007.

0.9.1006
- Root fix: AI ignores updated faction relations/power status, persistently uses outdated tone (threatening allies, bluffing while weak, doubling down when contradicted) — quadruple systemic fix:
  1. New rpg_state_anchor prompt node (Order 236), dynamically injects {{ world.current_faction_profile }} and {{ world.faction_settlement_summary }}, forcing AI to anchor to current faction relations and settlement power;
  2. rpg_state_anchor includes contradiction self-correction rules (three options: acknowledge & correct / personality-consistent explanation / in-character deflection), prohibiting holding positions that contradict facts;
  3. Modified character_persona section (any + rpg_dialogue + proactive_rpg): changed "maintain stable tone and consistent stance, no sudden persona reversal within a single turn" to "maintain stable core personality, but attitude must adjust promptly when relations/power/situation change; continuing to use outdated tone when conditions have changed is a roleplay failure";
  4. Added [State Anchor] paragraph to RPG channel character_persona: "Persona is not armor — keep core personality stable, but when relations/power/situation change, attitude must adjust accordingly".
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1006.

0.9.1005
- Root fix: AI characters stubbornly maintain hostility/pride even under extreme survival needs (e.g., throwing food away and mocking the provider while severely malnourished) — triple systemic fix:
  1. BuildStyleGuidelines prisoner branch: added "survival instinct overrides pride" rule — never reject/discard survival provisions under extreme need;
  2. hostile (socialIdentity + relationshipStatus): changed from absolute hardline to conditional hardline — when the player meets basic needs, the NPC may show reluctant, limited softening; no longer escalate hostility toward someone actively helping them survive;
  3. New rpg_survival_instinct prompt node (Order 236): defines extreme need thresholds (food<15%, rest<10%, health<30%), behavior rules (no rejecting/discarding survival provisions, no escalating hostility toward helpers, allow verbal stubbornness with honest body behavior), and minimal goodwill floor after needs ease.
- Added: rpg_survival_instinct node registered in SchemaCatalog, PromptUnifiedDefaults fallback, and PromptPersistenceService rendering branch.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1005.

0.9.1004

- Root fix: New node Order value was 1000 (default), placed after thought_chain(9999) causing incorrect position — assigned Order 235/236 for 4 new nodes, placed after response_contract(230) and before thought_chain(9999).
- Root fix: BuildStyleGuidelines ignored personalityTraits variable — added AppendTraitStyleGuidelines method, generating concrete dialogue behavior constraints for 15 key traits (Masochist, Kind, Bloodlust, Psychopath, etc.) and 2 contradictory trait pairs.

0.9.1000
- Root fix: Severe frame drops when opening comms console dialogue — Log.Warning in DoWindowContents for windowPos==0,0 fires every frame (inRect is window-local coords, x=y=0 is expected for centered windows), causing 60 stack traces + disk I/O per second blocking the main thread. Fix: removed the faulty check. Also fixed layout cache invalidation loop in DrawMessages — when typewriter animation is active, cache miss → InvalidateLayoutCache → rebuild → miss again in an infinite loop every frame. Fix: compute layout inline on cache miss instead of invalidating the entire cache.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.1000.

0.9.997
- Root fix: VehiclePawn (Vehicles Framework) inheriting Pawn causes RimTalk PersonaService.GetPersonality → AddHediff native crash — VehiclePawn inherits Pawn but lacks story/skills/health subsystems; when misidentified as RPG dialogue target, RimTalk's Hediff_Persona.GetOrAddNew calls AddHediff on it, triggering Unity engine-level crash (C# try-catch cannot capture). Fix: capability-based whitelist hybrid strategy that excludes Pawn subclasses lacking RPG dialogue capability at the entry point — ① PawnDialogueRoutingPolicy.IsRpgDialogueEligibleRace now fast-paths Humanlike/Mechanoid, and requires pawn.story!=null && pawn.skills!=null for ToolUser ② PawnDialogueCompDefInjector.IsEligiblePawnDef adds race.Humanlike/race.IsMechanoid/race.ToolUser whitelist filter. This automatically defends against any future Pawn subclass lacking story/skills (e.g. drones, vehicles) without per-type-name blacklisting.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.997.

0.9.996
- Root fix: "Letter_0" duplicate key crashes when loading old saves — legacy save ChoiceLetter subclasses had loadID=0, causing LoadedObjectDirectory.RegisterLoaded to throw "An item with the same key has already been added. Key: Letter_0". Fix: create Harmony Prefix patch LoadedObjectDirectoryPatch_FixLegacyLetterLoadID that checks loadID of the two ChoiceLetter subclasses before RegisterLoaded; if ≤0, uses new static AssignNextUniqueLoadID() method to allocate unique IDs; removes internal ExposeData fix logic from ChoiceLetters to prevent lagging repair.
- Fix: RPG archive compression channel output_specification self-contradicting repair infinite loop — add expectedText.Length == 0 check, preventing sections that correctly inherit from parent "any" channel from being flagged for repair, stopping infinite fix-save-reload cycles.
- Build: clean up Build.ps1 script, remove stale net48 subdirectory output, unify DLL output path.
- Tools: add Windows reserved device name "nul" to .gitignore, preventing normal file operations from failing.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.996.

0.9.995
- Root fix: Chatting with sleeping/downed pawns causes native crash — RestUtility.Awake(target) only checks whether the pawn's current Job is a sleep Job, not target.Downed. A downed but non-sleeping pawn (e.g., just incapacitated in combat) bypasses the check, and PawnCacheRenderer.RenderPawn crashes Unity when rendering a pawn in lying-down pose. Fix: 5-layer defense — ①CompPawnDialogue.CanShowRpgDialogueOption adds target.Downed check to block right-click menu ②JobDriver_RPGPawnDialogue FailOn adds target.Downed to immediately fail the Job ③JobDriver_RPGPawnDialogue openDialogue adds target.Downed check before opening ④DialogueContextResolver.IsPawnValid adds !pawn.Downed to global validation layer ⑤ChoiceLetter_PawnRpgInitiatedDialogue.TryOpenDialogue adds Downed+Awake check for NPC push path.
- Fix: Airdrop trade error "MakeThing error: Apparel_Broadwrap is madeFromStuff but stuff=null" — BuildStacks method passed stuff=null for MadeFromStuff=true ThingDefs, causing ThingMaker.MakeThing to error. Fix: when def.MadeFromStuff, use def.defaultStuff as the default material.
- Version: bumped About/About.xml modVersion to 0.9.995.

0.9.48
- Added: ransom prisoner selector upgraded to multi-select with `Select All / Clear All / Confirm`; default selection is none to prevent accidental mass payment.
- Added: after selecting multiple prisoners via `request_info(prisoner)`, diplomacy now emits a batch prisoner dossier (list + total ask + total offer window) and injects a batch reference block for same-turn AI negotiation.
- Added: batch ransom execution constraints without introducing new action names: still uses `pay_prisoner_ransom`; when batch context exists and payment is emitted this turn, the response must cover all selected targets exactly once and keep total offer within the batch window. Missing/duplicate/unexpected/out-of-window targets now fail fast.
- Changed: batch execution is serial first-failure-stop; successful targets are not rolled back and are removed from the pending batch set, so subsequent turns only need to cover remaining targets.
- Added: `FactionDialogueSession` now persists batch-ransom runtime state (batch id, target set, total ask/window) with old-save compatibility.
- Added: `RansomContractRecord` now stores `IsBatchRansom/BatchGroupId/BatchTargetCount` metadata for downstream penalty branching.
- Changed: fixed medium-relaxed policy for batch penalties: release deadline +50%, drop-rate thresholds relaxed, and normal timeout/drop penalties scaled by 0.7.
- Kept strict: organ-loss penalties remain full single-target strength even in batch mode; no batch scaling is applied to organ-loss punishment.
- Prompting: synchronized `action_rules`, system prompt policy, and retry contract hints with new `[RansomBatchSelection]` rules to avoid single-submit-only outputs in batch context.
- Localization: added EN/ZH keys for batch-ransom UI and system feedback (coverage mismatch, total-window violation, remaining targets, select all/clear all, etc.).

- Fixed: `ItemAirdropIntentParser` now supports delimiter boundaries (`| / \\ 、，。；：`) and mixed alpha-digit-CJK splitting (for example `steel10个`) with quantity/unit noise filtering.
- Added: local CN/EN synonym expansion in `ThingDefResolver` (runs before AI alias expansion), plus a strong-match score channel for normalized defName/label containment.
- Added: candidate diagnostics counters (`recordsScanned`, `rejectedByBlacklist`, `rejectedByBlockedCategory`, `rejectedByFamily`, `rejectedByMatchScore`) and `nearMisses` sampling.
- Observability: `RequestItemAirdrop.Stage` now includes full diagnostics in both `prepare` and `failed` stages (tokens/family/aliases/rejection counters/top near-miss).

0.7.90
- Root fix: fully removed the external `persona_bootstrap` request path from `GameComponent_RPGManager.PersonaBootstrap`; no more `SendChatRequestAsync(... PersonaBootstrap)` calls are made.
- Changed: `ProcessNpcPersonaBootstrapTick` is now RimTalk-only. Without RimTalk, bootstrap completes immediately (fail-fast); with RimTalk, only persona copy/sync logic runs.
- Changed: `ProcessNpcPersonaRuntimeTick` now hard-disables runtime scanning when RimTalk is unavailable, preventing repeated no-op scans.
- Changed: `RetryOrFallbackPersonaPrompt` now only attempts RimTalk sync/copy. It no longer retries AI persona generation and no longer writes local fallback persona text.
- Compatibility: kept save fields `npcPersonaBootstrapCompleted` and `npcPersonaBootstrapVersion`; bumped bootstrap behavior version to `3` so old saves auto-converge to the new behavior.
- Docs: synchronized `doc/Index.md`, `doc/Api.md`, and `doc/config.md`.
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.7.90`.

0.7.89
- Improved: `request_item_airdrop` now prioritizes natural-language normalization, instead of requiring fixed family keywords on the first pass.
- Improved: added a first-pass AI alias expansion stage (configurable). When candidates are empty, the system requests CN/EN `aliases` and re-runs retrieval with those terms.
- Improved: when family is known but candidates are empty, added one same-family relaxed retry (category-block filtering only) without cross-family fallback.
- Improved: boosted exact Def-hit ranking (defName/label exact matches), so explicit requests like `steel` prefer the matching ThingDef.
- Added config surface: `EnableAirdropAliasExpansion`, `ItemAirdropAliasExpansionMaxCount`, `ItemAirdropAliasExpansionTimeoutSeconds`, and `EnableAirdropSameFamilyRelaxedRetry` with EN/ZH settings labels.
- Prompt contract: `request_item_airdrop` guidance now asks for CN/EN aliases in `constraints` on the first request to improve hit rate.
- Validation: `build.ps1` passed (0 errors; existing Scriban `NU1902/NU1903` security warnings remain).
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.7.89`.

- Fixed: candidate construction now enforces strict family-first behavior; once a family is identified, cross-family fallback candidates are no longer merged into phase-2 selection.

0.7.87

- Added: dedicated airdrop domain modules: `ItemAirdropModels`, `ItemAirdropIntentParser`, `ItemAirdropSafetyPolicy`, and `ItemAirdropSelectionParser`.
- Added: whitelist-first candidate strategy (`food/medicine/weapon/apparel`) with generic fallback pool, ranked by `match score > safety score > price`.

0.7.83
- Fix: unified diplomacy input-host lifecycle so the input box stays read-only until the full AI pipeline settles, including main reply, image requests, NPC typewriter playback, and the follow-up strategy suggestion request.
- Root cause: the previous diplomacy input lock only treated `IsHardBlocked` as read-only, while the strategy follow-up phase lived in `IsSoftBlocked`, so Windows IME could reattach to a freshly recreated Unity text host before it was stable.
- Added: `RimChat/UI/Dialog_DiplomacyDialogue.InputLifecycle.cs` to centralize diplomacy input-host ownership and the short reactivation stabilization window.
- Changed: `Dialog_DiplomacyDialogue.DrawInputArea(...)` now routes both `IsHardBlocked` and `IsSoftBlocked` through the read-only gate; `IsInputLockedByAiTurn(...)` and `IsWaitingForNpcTurn(...)` now include strategy follow-up and stabilization checks.
- Validation: `build.ps1` passed (`0 errors`, existing Scriban security warnings remain), then `run.ps1` completed deployment and launched the game.
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.7.83`.

0.7.82
- Fix: `PromptPersistenceService.WorkbenchComposer.ResolveWorkspaceContextEnvironmentText(...)` no longer emits the `{{ runtime.environment }}` placeholder for `rpg_archive_compression` and `summary_generation`; it now returns the literal `No environment context.` text.
- Root cause: compression/summary channels do not build a full runtime environment object, but the prompt context still carried `runtime.environment`, which triggered RimTalk native Scriban errors (`Object runtime is null`).
- Short-term block: prevents unresolved runtime placeholder tokens from entering the native render stage and removes this recurring `Player.log` error.
- Validation: `build.ps1` passed (`0 errors`, existing Scriban security warnings remain).

- Improved: section editing now uses `PromptWorkbenchChipEditor`, so valid variable tokens render again as highlighted chips; variables inserted from the browser immediately appear in chip form inside the editor.
- Improved: the preview panel now uses a read-only chip-highlight view so section text and aggregate preview share the same token highlighting, and the editor footer now shows live Scriban/variable validation status.
- Validation: ran `build.ps1` to verify chip editing, highlighted preview rendering, and live validation in the prompt workspace.
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.7.2`.

0.7.0
- Refactor: finalized Prompt Compat as a load/import-only legacy shell. `RimChatSettings` now keeps only native `PromptSectionCatalog` plus summary/persona/bridge live fields; old `EnableRimTalkPromptCompat`, `CompatTemplate`, `RimTalkDiplomacy`, and `RimTalkRpg` no longer participate in save output or stable UI.
- Added: `PromptSectionSchemaCatalog`, `PromptSectionAggregateBuilder`, and `PromptPersistenceService.SectionAggregates`; diplomacy and RPG mainline prompts now build one canonical `root channel -> prompt channel -> 8 sections` aggregate and insert it exactly once into the hierarchical builder.
- Added: `Prompt/Default/PromptSectionCatalog_Default.json` as the canonical default asset entry point, with a one-version fallback read of the old `RimTalkPromptEntries_Default.json`.
- Added: `LegacyPromptMigrationReport` / `LegacyPromptMigrationEntry` plus overwrite-style report output at `Prompt/Reports/LegacyPromptMigrationReport.json`; settings, preset, bundle, and custom-store legacy imports now share the same report + Player.log summary path.
- Changed: the Prompt tab is now the stable section-driven workspace with fixed `root channel -> prompt channel -> sectionId` navigation and preview from the current canonical aggregate; entry/compat/workbench editing paths are no longer part of the stable flow.
- Changed: the RimTalk page is now limited to `Bridge / Variables / Summary & Persona`; the variable browser now uses one neutral shared model (`path / scope / sourceId / sourceLabel / availability / description`) across Prompt and RimTalk UIs.
- Cleanup: removed the standalone `Dialog_PromptWorkbench` path. Old "Prompt Workbench" naming remains only as compatibility shell text keys, not as a separate entry-driven editor.
- Validation: `build.ps1` completed successfully and stayed on the baseline (`1 warning`, `0 errors`).
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.7.0`.

0.6.35
- Refactor: continued collapsing the RimTalk prompt compatibility layer into import/migration-only behavior; `Prompt/Custom`, presets, bundles, and variable catalogs now persist native `PromptSectionCatalog + provider` state instead of storing `RimTalkDiplomacy / RimTalkRpg / CompatTemplate` as live runtime configuration.
- Added: `RimTalkVariableProvider` and `RimTalkMemoryPatchVariableProvider` now expose the first real bridged variable set; legacy `{{context}}`, `{{prompt}}`, `{{chat.history}}`, `{{chat.history_simplified}}`, and `{{json.format}}` now auto-migrate into `pawn.rimtalk.*`, `dialogue.rimtalk.*`, and `system.rimtalk.*`.
- Added: RimTalk API registered context/pawn/environment variables now map automatically into `dialogue.rimtalk.*`, `pawn.rimtalk.*`, and `world.rimtalk.*`; variable browser and picker now show source labels and runtime dependency-missing state.
- Changed: preset import, preset-store load, bundle import, and RPG custom-store load now auto-read legacy compat fields and migrate them into the native section catalog; old bundle modules `rimtalk_diplomacy / rimtalk_rpg` are folded into the new `RpgPrompt` import path.
- Changed: prompt bundle export no longer includes RimTalk legacy modules, and preset/bundle/custom-store output no longer writes legacy compat channel fields.
- Localization: added EN/CN keys for variable source labels, dependency status, and RimTalk bridge variable descriptions.
- Validation: `build.ps1` completed build + deploy successfully (`1 warning`, `0 errors`).

0.6.34
- Refactor: introduced `PromptSectionCatalog` as the native authoritative section model so settings, `Prompt/Custom`, presets, and bundles now persist prompt sections as `channel -> section -> text` instead of treating `PromptEntries` / `CompatTemplate` as live runtime state.
- Changed: `PromptEntryStaticTextCatalog` now resolves diplomacy `dialogue.diplomacy_dialogue.*` texts from the normalized section catalog, removing the last hard binding to static compat-era constants in the runtime prompt path.
- Added: legacy migration now imports old `PromptEntries` / `CompatTemplate` payloads into the native section model exactly once; unknown bare variables and polluted rendered prompts (`<prompt_context>`, `=== PREVIEW DIAGNOSTICS ===`, `[FILE]`, `[CODE]`, etc.) are rejected and reset back to default sections.
- Changed: settings, RPG custom store, preset payloads, and bundle transfer now normalize `PromptSectionCatalog` first and then clear legacy compat fields, leaving compat structures as import-only DTOs instead of active runtime storage.
- Logging: migration failures and bad-data cleanup now report to `Player.log` only, with no extra in-game report window or local file report.
- Validation: `build.ps1` completed build + deploy successfully (`1 warning`, `0 errors`); GitNexus `detect_changes(scope=all)` flagged the change set as `critical`, and the implementation was kept centralized on the native section catalog path.
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` mod version to `0.6.34`.

0.6.33

- Added: introduced `IPromptRuntimeVariableProvider`, a shared variable registry, and core/external provider scaffolding so template validation, variable catalogs, the variable browser, and runtime rendering share one canonical namespaced variable source.
- Changed: `RimTalkChannelCompatConfig` no longer auto-rebuilds `CompatTemplate` from `PromptEntries`; legacy payloads are now migrated and sanitized on load instead of being written back into the live runtime chain.
- Changed: prompt custom store, preset persistence, and bundle save flows now scrub legacy `EnableRimTalkPromptCompat` / `RimTalkCompatTemplate` fields; bundle exports no longer include RimTalk legacy modules by default.
- Changed: the old Prompt Workbench launcher now routes back to the stable Prompt page so entry-driven editing can no longer write legacy prompt structures into the active workflow.
- Validation: `build.ps1` completed build + deploy successfully (`1 warning`, `0 errors`).

0.6.17
- Fixed: root cause was cross-mod Scriban ABI conflict (Steam mod 3551203752 loads `Scriban.dll` 1.0.0.0 first); `ScribanPromptEngine` is now refactored with runtime capability probing + reflection-based diagnostics extraction, removing hard binding to newer APIs (`EnableRelaxed*` / `LogMessageBag`) while preserving strict render semantics.
- Fixed: `GameComponent_RPGManager.PersonaBootstrap` now builds persona-bootstrap prompts through strict Scriban rendering (`PromptTemplateRenderer.RenderOrThrow(...)`) instead of string `Replace` chains.
- Fixed: RimTalk persona-copy render failure/empty result no longer gets swallowed-and-skipped; it now throws `PromptRenderException` and interrupts the current chain (no silent fallback).
- Fixed: RimTalk template editors now show realtime Scriban diagnostics for entry content, channel template, and persona-copy template (error code + line/column + unknown-variable status).
- Docs: removed old bridge/raw-fallback wording in `spec/Index.md` and `Api.md`, unified to strict Scriban runtime contract.
- Validation: added acceptance-loop records in Scriban migration docs (build gate + invalid-template blocking regression + historical-template migration regression), and synced About/About.xml, VersionLog.txt, VersionLog_en.txt, Api.md, and spec/Index.md.
0.6.16
- Breaking continuation: removed legacy `PromptTemplateRenderer.Render(...)` entrypoints; mainline now enforces explicit `RenderOrThrow + PromptRenderContext`.
- Strict runtime: removed legacy prompt-entry fallback assembly and policy-node hardcoded fallbacks in `PromptPersistenceService.Hierarchical`; missing templates now throw `TemplateMissing (1201)`.
- Image channel: migrated `send_image` caption fallback from string substitution to Scriban strict rendering; render failure/empty output now throws and aborts.
- Migration engine: extended `PromptTemplateAutoRewriteResult` with per-template diagnostics (success/failure/reason); schema-upgrade throw now includes first blocked template reason.
- Editor validation: upgraded template validation to Scriban compile diagnostics (error code + line/column + message), replacing variable-only manual checks.
- Cleanup: physically removed `RimTalkCompatBridge` runtime implementation files, keeping only compatibility model definitions.
- Docs: synchronized `doc/scriban_engine_migration.md`, `Api.md`, `config.md`, and `spec/Index.md` to strict no-fallback contract.

0.6.15
- Breaking change: prompt rendering mainline is now unified to `IScribanPromptEngine.RenderOrThrow(...)`; prompt render failures throw `PromptRenderException` and no silent/raw-text fallback is allowed.
- Architecture cleanup: environment `SceneEntries` template rendering is migrated from legacy regex replacement to strict Scriban render; unknown variables are blocked with `UnknownVariable`.
- Runtime decoupling: active runtime path no longer invokes `RimTalkCompatBridge` render APIs; settings variable browser now reads local namespaced snapshot from `PromptVariableCatalog`.
- Performance and observability: added fixed-capacity LRU compiled-template cache and render telemetry in Scriban engine; API debug window now shows cache hit-rate, hit/miss/eviction counts, and average parse/render latency.
- Localization: added EN/CN key `RimChat_ApiDebugScribanTelemetry`.
- Documentation: added `doc/scriban_engine_migration.md` (namespace rules + error-code table) and synced `Api.md`, `config.md`, and `spec/Index.md`.

- Compatibility: no save schema or prompt-file format changes; old saves and legacy prompt files remain compatible.
- Changed: bumped version to 0.5.28 and synced About/About.xml, VersionLog.txt, VersionLog_en.txt, and spec/Index.md.

0.5.22
- Added: minimal 3-mode image API convergence: `sync_url`, `sync_payload`, and `async_job`, so one implementation can cover most third-party image sources.
- Changed: aligned Image API tab UI/UX with the main API tab interaction style (selector-driven options + placeholders + status color feedback).
- Added: Image API connectivity test button (same UX as API tab), with sync/async probe paths and auth-failure reporting.
- Changed: Image API connectivity test now uses coroutine-based async requests instead of blocking probe loops.
- Fixed: non-ARK image providers now retry once without `size` on first-attempt 5xx or size-related errors, improving compatibility with SiliconFlow-style OpenAI endpoints.
- Fixed: `SiliconFlow` image preset now uses OpenAI Images payload shape for `/v1/images/generations`, preventing ARK-only fields from causing provider-side 500 errors.
- Improved: ComfyUI async submit now surfaces a clear localized error when `ckpt_name` fails validation (`not in list`), guiding users to set an existing checkpoint filename.
- Changed: Image API tab is now provider-preset driven (Volcengine ARK / OpenAI-compatible / SiliconFlow / local ComfyUI / Custom), with auto-filled endpoint/mode/auth defaults to reduce setup complexity.
- Added: advanced image options are now hidden by default and shown only for `Custom` preset (mode/auth/path/polling overrides).
- Added: persistent image API fields (`Mode/SchemaPreset/AuthMode/ResponseUrlPath/ResponseB64Path/Async*Path/Poll*`) with old-save-safe defaults.
- Added: `SchemaPreset=comfyui` now auto-switches to `async_job` and supports ComfyUI flow (`/prompt` submit -> `/history/{job_id}` poll -> `/view` fetch).
- Added: synchronous image parsing now supports both URL and Base64 payloads with common-path fallbacks (`url`, `data[0].url`, `b64_json`, etc.).
- Added: auth modes now support `bearer/api_key_header/query_key/none`, including custom header/query key names.
- Localization: added EN/CN keys for the new image-mode controls in the Image API tab.
- Compatibility: `send_image` action contract and prompt-file schema remain unchanged; old saves and legacy prompt files stay readable.
- Changed: bumped version to 0.5.22 and synced About/About.xml, VersionLog.txt, VersionLog_en.txt, spec/Index.md, Api.md, and config.md.

0.5.21
- Added: a new left-bottom `History` button in manual RPG dialogue; clicking it opens a centered history panel in the blank area above the dialogue box (current session only).
- Added: session history now renders full dialogue details in chronological order and inlines triggered action outcomes under the related NPC turn (`action name + success/failure/error + reason`).
- Added: the history panel can be opened anytime (including typing/waiting states); clicking outside the panel closes only the panel and no longer closes the RPG dialogue window.
- Kept: existing right-bottom quick history pagination remains unchanged as a shortcut.
- Localization: added EN/CN keys for history panel labels, empty state, action result labels, and reason prefix.
- Compatibility: runtime-only UI/history additions; no save schema or prompt-file format changes, old saves and legacy prompt files remain compatible.

0.5.16
- Added: Prompt -> Faction Prompts now supports Add/Remove template actions. New templates can bind to any FactionDef, including mod factions.
- Rule: one template per faction. If a template already exists for the selected faction, the UI auto-selects that template instead of creating a duplicate.
- Rule: only user-added custom templates can be removed. Default templates (from Prompt/Default/FactionPrompts_Default.json) are protected from removal.
- Compatibility: removed custom templates are no longer auto-recreated on load; imported configs still auto-fill protected default templates.
- Compatibility: templates for missing mod factions are preserved and marked as Missing, so old saves and prompt files do not lose data.
- Localization: added EN/CN keys for add/remove actions, default-removal blocking hint, missing-faction tag, and existing-template auto-select feedback.

0.5.15
- Fixed: Image API tab now uses full-page vertical scrolling so the image template editor remains fully reachable on smaller resolutions (ID/name/description/text/add/delete).
- Added: runtime-only counter `FactionDialogueSession.pendingImageRequests` (not serialized) to unify send-image waiting-state gating.
- Changed: `send_image` now increments pending image count at request start and decrements on callback (success/failure), with non-negative protection and old-save compatibility.
- Changed: diplomacy input lock now uses one gate: AI request pending OR image request pending OR active NPC typewriter; button send and keyboard send share this same gate.
- Fixed: conversation-ended state now has higher priority; ended sessions show only end-reason status (no typing indicator), while late image callbacks can still append to message history.

0.3.129

0.3.128

- Changed: `FactionPromptManager` no longer probes or migrates custom faction-prompt JSON from the legacy config path and reads only from the unified current path.
- Changed: RPG NPC archive JSON no longer accepts the old top-level `turns` shape, LeaderMemory JSON no longer accepts legacy uppercase/alternate key names, and neither data set auto-migrates JSON files from legacy directories anymore.

0.3.127
- Changed: `PromptPersistenceService` now loads system-prompt config JSON through the typed codec only; incomplete or failed typed parses are rejected instead of falling back to the old hand-written parser.
- Changed: diplomacy strategy-suggestion payloads no longer expose legacy alias fields such as `ShortLabel`, `TriggerBasis`, or `HiddenReply`.

0.3.126
- Changed: after a full dialogue JSON-chain audit, the diplomacy parser no longer accepts legacy top-level `action/parameters/response` wrappers or alternate action keys such as `action_type/name/type`; only the `{\"actions\":[...]}` contract remains valid.
- Changed: the RPG parser no longer reads visible dialogue from JSON `text/response` fields; visible dialogue must stay outside the parser-facing JSON block.
- Changed: both diplomacy and RPG reduced-context retries now append strict contract reminders so fallback requests do not drift back to old JSON shapes.
- Fixed: RPG history normalization no longer writes raw JSON payloads back into visible chat history when the model violates the contract.

0.3.125
- Changed: RPG now uses one strict output contract only: natural dialogue text plus an optional trailing `{\"actions\":[...]}` JSON object. The default prompt explicitly forbids legacy top-level `action/content/text` wrappers.
- Changed: reduced-context RPG retries now append a strict protocol reminder so the retry path keeps the same output format instead of drifting to an older JSON shape.
- Changed: the RPG parser no longer accepts legacy top-level `action` payloads and now reads gameplay effects only from the `actions` array contract.

0.3.124
- Fixed: the RPG parser now accepts legacy `{\"action\":\"say\",\"content\":\"...\"}` / `message` payloads and treats them as dialogue text, so they no longer trigger `Unknown RPG action ignored: say`.
- Fixed: retryable RPG `HTTP 400 user input rejected / Param Incorrect` responses are now logged as retry warnings instead of terminal errors when RimChat can recover with reduced context.

0.3.123
- Changed: the RPG pawn persona bootstrap template now uses the new `He/She is a [core temperament] ...` sentence structure, and the provided Template / Example pair is shipped as the default persona-generation prompt.
- Changed: NPC persona bootstrap now reads its system/user/template/example text from `Prompt/Default/RpgPrompts_Default.json`, so future template edits no longer require touching C# literals.
- Changed: persona normalization and fallback text were updated for the new template and now emit consistent `He/She/They` pronouns based on pawn gender.

0.3.122
- Fixed: added required default `description` and `label` fields to the new visible RPG memory defs (`RimChat_PleasantChatMemory`, `RimChat_DeepConversationMemory`, `RimChat_SlightedMemory`), removing the RimWorld config error "affects mood but doesn't have a description" so the memories load and appear correctly on the pawn card.
- Fixed: RPG `TryGainMemory` no longer incorrectly requires `thoughtClass` to be explicitly populated; both explicit `Thought_Memory` defs and vanilla mood memories that rely on the default thought class now pass validation.
- Fixed: the first RPG reply no longer appears blank when the model returns pure JSON such as `{ \"text\": \"...\", \"actions\": [...] }`; the parser now reads `text` / `response` fields from the JSON body.
- Fixed: the visible RPG memory DefInjected localization keys now target `stages.0.label/description`, resolving missing-language-key text on the pawn card.
- Fixed: the RPG parser now strips malformed action markers such as `**<TryGainMemory>**` and their tiny action payloads from displayed dialogue so parser-facing junk no longer leaks into natural-language chat.

0.3.121
- Fixed: RPG prompt assembly now reloads prompt text from `Prompt/Default/RpgPrompts_Default.json` and `Prompt/Custom/RpgPrompts_Custom.json` before building, preventing stale in-memory RPG API prompts from ignoring updated default files at runtime.
- Fixed: the RPG prompt assembly path now resolves role-setting, format-constraint, action-reliability, and `ApiActionPrompt` directly from `RpgPrompts_Custom.json` / `RpgPrompts_Default.json` instead of treating cached `RimChatSettings` fields as the final source of truth.
- Fixed: `RpgApiActionPromptConfig.CreateFallback()` still contained older `TryGainMemory` / compact prompt strings that had drifted from `Prompt/Default/RpgPrompts_Default.json`, causing fallback/normalization paths to pull the settings UI back to stale text. The fallback literals now match the JSON defaults.
- Fixed: `TryGainMemory` previously defaulted to social-opinion thoughts such as `Chitchat`, `DeepTalk`, and `Slighted`, which usually do not appear in the pawn mood memory card. Those legacy tokens now remap to visible RPG memory defs (plus `KindWordsMood` / `InsultedMood`), and the default RPG prompt examples were updated accordingly.

0.3.120
- Changed: diplomacy default prompts now use a single "in-character dialogue + one raw `{\"actions\":[...]}` JSON object" contract instead of the legacy single `action/parameters/response` template.
- Changed: `SystemPrompt_Default.json` now keeps diplomacy-only templates; RPG role-setting, format-constraint, action-reliability, and opening-objective defaults are sourced from `Prompt/Default/RpgPrompts_Default.json` to avoid diplomacy/RPG rule bleed.
- Changed: diplomacy exit handling now uses a graded policy; low-information input gets a short reply first, while repeated low-information or clear harassment escalates to `exit_dialogue`, `go_offline`, or `set_dnd`.
- Changed: diplomacy prompts now explicitly allow parser-facing structured JSON while keeping natural-language dialogue free of AI-identity and game-mechanics mentions, and unavailable features are declined with in-world reasons.
- Changed: diplomacy decision policy, public-post restraint, `reject_request` action boundary, quest wording, and output-language guidance were tightened to reduce hostility overreach and protocol drift.
- Changed: prompt policy schema was bumped to `3`; default budgets, protected nodes, and trim priorities were rebalanced so `response_contract` and `quest_guidance` are less likely to disappear.
- Changed: RPG no-action reliability guidance now aligns on a two-turn no-effect threshold before adding `TryGainMemory`, matching the prompt policy threshold.
- Docs: synced `README.md`, `Api.md`, and `config.md` with the diplomacy/RPG prompt split and the new output contract.

0.3.119

0.3.117

0.3.116

- Changed: fixed diplomacy API costs now align with vanilla values for `request_caravan` (-15) and `request_aid` (-25 for Military / Medical / Resources), while `create_quest` now always applies a fixed -10 goodwill cost on success.
- Improved: diplomacy prompt rules now explicitly forbid using `adjust_goodwill` to duplicate the built-in goodwill costs of `request_caravan`, `request_aid`, and `create_quest`.
- Improved: successful diplomacy actions now write richer faction-memory event text, including fixed goodwill cost records and quest issuance memory, for better later recall.

- Fixed: diplomacy window close now explicitly cancels both the main reply request and strategy follow-up request to avoid post-close writes into stale sessions.

0.3.112
- Fixed: RPG session compression is now triggered only after session finalization (`FinalizeSession`), never during active turn recording.
- Fixed: added `isFinalized` session field to prevent active-session miscompression and to treat legacy data as finalized by default.

- Fixed: compression success callback now rechecks finalized/retained-session guards to avoid race-condition compression of the latest full session.

0.3.111

- Added: RPG window lifecycle now carries `sessionId` per dialogue and finalizes archive session on window close.
- Added: session-level strict LLM compression policy: keep only the latest session with `turnCount >= 2` as full turns; compress others to one-sentence summaries.
- Added: compression failure now keeps original turns (`summary_failed`) and retries incrementally on touch/read/save with cooldown throttling.
- Changed: NPC personal memory injection now reads compressed historical session summaries first, then injects details from the retained full session only.
- Changed: unresolved-intent extraction now only reads the retained full session turns to avoid stale compressed-history noise.

- Changed: Added shared renderer path for node-body placeholders (`{{api_limits_body}}`, `{{quest_guidance_body}}`, `{{response_contract_body}}`) with legacy output-preserving defaults.
- Changed: Default template JSON and legacy PromptTemplates serializer/parser were synced with the new wrapper fields.
0.3.65
- Added: Expanded `PromptTemplates` with channel-role and RPG contract templates (`DiplomacyFallbackRoleTemplate`, `RpgRoleSettingTemplate`, `RpgCompactFormatConstraintTemplate`, `RpgActionReliabilityRuleTemplate`).
- Changed: Hierarchical prompt builder now reads diplomacy fallback role text and RPG role-setting text from templates with placeholder rendering, while preserving old hardcoded fallback behavior.
- Changed: RPG format constraint and action reliability rule now support template-driven rendering, reducing hardcoded prompt text in the builder.
- Changed: Default `SystemPrompt_Default.json` and legacy JSON serializer/parser for `PromptTemplates` are synced with the new fields.
0.3.64
- Added: Introduced `PromptTemplateTextConfig` to externalize shared prompt text sections (`FactGroundingTemplate`, `OutputLanguageTemplate`) into runtime/default config.
- Added: New placeholder renderer `PromptTemplateRenderer` with `{{variable}}` syntax support for reusable prompt templates.
- Changed: Hierarchical prompt builder now renders `fact_grounding` and `output_language` from config templates first, with legacy hardcoded text kept as fallback.
- Changed: Prompt config JSON default template now includes `PromptTemplates` block; legacy serializer/parser and typed codec normalization are both updated for compatibility.
0.3.60
- Changed: Removed bidirectional default-template sync buttons from prompt settings (Apply Default To Runtime / Write Runtime To Default).
- Changed: Removed default-template sync APIs from PromptPersistenceService (GetDefaultTemplatePath, ReloadRuntimeConfigFromDefaultTemplate, SaveRuntimeConfigToDefaultTemplate).
- Updated: Removed related CN/EN localization keys and synced docs (README.md, Api.md, config.md).
0.3.59
- Fixed: Dialogue token parsing now scopes extraction to the response usage object to avoid false matches from assistant text.
- Added: Usage extraction now supports multiple schema aliases (prompt_tokens/input_tokens/promptTokenCount, completion_tokens/output_tokens/candidatesTokenCount, total_tokens/totalTokenCount).
- Added: Automatic fallback to local estimate when provider usage is clearly inconsistent with request/response size; UI keeps the estimated marker.
- Preventive: Added provider-vs-estimate diagnostic logging for faster out.log triage.
0.3.58
- Fixed: Prompt runtime config persistence path moved to user config directory (`Config/RimChat/Prompt/Custom/system_prompt_config.json`) to prevent deploy overwrite loss.
- Added: Automatic migration for legacy prompt config files from old mod/save_data paths on first load.
- Changed: Default-template read now prefers user override file (`Config/RimChat/Prompt/Default/SystemPrompt_Default.json`); write-back now targets this persistent override path.
- Added: `build.ps1` now backs up/restores destination `Prompt/Custom` during deploy as an extra safety net for legacy data.

0.3.57

- Improved: Main strategy-missing path also attempts narrative fallback before issuing follow-up requests, reducing repeated `missing/invalid` loops.
- Changed: Strategy follow-up prompt no longer appends full recent dialogue history to reduce roleplay drift and improve structured-output compliance.

0.3.39
- Changed: Replaced linear prompt assembly in `BuildFullSystemPrompt` and `BuildRPGFullSystemPrompt` with hierarchical context builders.

- Added: Prompt default config field `UseHierarchicalPromptFormat: true`.

0.3.38
- Added: Introduced `DialogueContextCompressionService` for dynamic prompt history packing in diplomacy/RPG channels.
- Added: New staged compression policy: keep latest 15 full turns, compress turns beyond 15, and apply a second compression pass to recency window 40-50 when total turns exceed 50.
- Added: Compression mark model (`+1` per pass, max `+2`) with deferred rolling behavior when a segment would exceed mark limit.
- Changed: Diplomacy main request path now uses compressed context instead of fixed recent-window truncation.
- Changed: Strategy follow-up request now reuses the same compressed context builder to reduce token spikes in long sessions.
- Changed: RPG request path now sends compressed conversation context while preserving all system prompts.

0.3.36
- Changed: Project-wide rebrand from RimDiplomacy to RimChat (solution/project/module folder names, assembly name, root namespace, class/type identifiers, language key prefixes, Def names, and packageId).
- Changed: Build/deploy scripts and workspace paths updated to RimChat; build output DLL renamed to RimChat.dll.
- Compatibility: This is a deep rename and may not be backward-compatible with old save/config identifiers that depended on previous names.

Version Update Log
0.3.35
- Changed: `ExitDialogueCooldown` in RPG dialogue now applies a 1-day cooldown (60000 ticks), and action-definition prompt text is aligned.
- Added: RPG memory fallback now performs one 80% roll after dialogue reaches 5 rounds; on success it auto-adds `TryGainMemory` (mood-affecting memory buff).
- Improved: RPG system feedback now uses a translucent panel and shows cooldown remaining time, memory-roll result, and memory-application details.
- Adjusted: Removed Recruit auto-completion logic and kept model-native action output only.
0.3.34
- Changed: RPG API action instructions now use a shared dynamic definition block at runtime, removing the legacy RPGApiGuidelines fixed-injection path.
- Improved: Removed the legacy "API Guidelines" editor section from RPG settings, and preview now matches the same dynamic action-definition block used at runtime.
0.3.33
- Changed: When RPG API is enabled, runtime system prompt now always injects the AppendRPGApiDefinitions action-definition block and no longer appends legacy RPGApiGuidelines text.
0.3.32
- Improved: RPG dialogue job now performs high-frequency moving-target checks during pathing (every 15 ticks) and repaths immediately when target position changes, instead of mostly waiting for stale-cell arrival retries.
- Improved: Unified the dialogue-open distance threshold constant to reduce mismatch-induced pauses between follow and window-open checks.
0.3.31
- Fixed: Completed LeaderMemory JSON persistence fields by adding read/write support for lastDecayCheckTick, playerRelationValues, and FactionMemoryEntry.firstContactTick/lastMentionedTick/relationHistory.
- Fixed: Removed the extra 50-entry trim during leader-memory file write to avoid over-truncation on top of the in-memory 200-entry cap.
- Added: RPG dialogue now persists per NPC into independent files at save_data/<saveName>/rpg_npc_dialogues/npc_<pawnId>.json.
- Added: NPC archives are hydrated back into RPG runtime state (persona prompt, RPG relation values, cooldown-until tick) after load for better continuity.
0.3.30
- Added: New-save startup now seeds baseline memory snapshots for all non-player factions (goodwill + current relation kind), preventing empty first-contact memory.
- Added: Post-load takeover now backfills legacy `FactionDialogueSession.messages` into faction memory, enabling mid-save adoption.
- Added: Idempotent marker events (`init-snapshot` / `session-backfill`) to prevent duplicate imports on repeated loads.
- Improved: Missing 5-dimension relation seeds are auto-recovered from current goodwill after load for better old-save compatibility.
0.3.29
- Added: Implemented bidirectional RPG-Diplomacy memory pipeline (RPG depart summary + diplomacy session-close summary) into faction long-term memory.
- Added: Harmony patch on Pawn.ExitMap(bool, Rot4) with strict guards (non-player faction, humanlike, player-home map, recent RPG trace).
- Added: Diplomacy window now generates exactly one session summary on close only when new messages were added.
- Added: RPG prompt now injects shared faction dynamic memory block without overwriting pawn persona (20 pool cap, 6 injected items, 2200-char budget).
- Added: Summary strategy is rule-first with low-confidence LLM fallback; if AI is unavailable it safely keeps rule summaries.
- Fixed: Corrected leader-memory JSON field mapping mismatch and added backward-compatible parsing for new cross-channel summary fields.
0.3.28
- Added: API settings now show "Recent dialogue token usage: xxxx (Low/Medium/High)" at the bottom.
- Added: Last dialogue token snapshot for Diplomacy and RPG channels (prompt/completion/total, channel, timestamp).
- Added: Usage parsing now prefers response usage fields, with fallback estimation from request+response text (4 chars 鈮?1 token) and estimated marker.
- Added: New CN/EN language keys RimChat_LastDialogueTokenUsage* and RimChat_TokenLevel*.
0.3.27
- Fixed: RPG dialogue job now refreshes moving-target alignment by looping back to follow until interaction distance is actually reached.
- Fixed: Added pre-open validation (same map/spawned/in-range) to prevent misaligned dialogue window triggers.
- Improved: Added reachability fail condition to reduce invalid executions when the target keeps moving.
0.3.26

- Fixed: TryGainMemory failure feedback now includes valid defName examples for faster correction.

0.5.23

0.5.25

- Compatibility: Added migration for legacy ComfyUI polling settings; historical default of 60 attempts is auto-raised to 180.
- Changed: ComfyUI Local preset now enforces a minimum of 180 polling attempts to avoid premature timeout on slower local generation.
