0.6.4
- Refactor: Prompt Workbench `Diplomacy` and `RPG` channels now use the same entry workflow as RimTalk (`list + entry editor` with Name/Role/Position/InChatDepth/Enabled/Content).
- Runtime: diplomacy/RPG final system prompt is now assembled by concatenating only enabled entries in order, rendered through the RimTalk Scriban path.
- Compatibility: added a "new entries -> legacy fields" backfill layer; save/export now auto-syncs legacy fields in `SystemPrompt_Custom.json` and `PawnDialoguePrompt_Custom.json` so old saves/prompt files remain readable.
- Migration: when only legacy prompt fields exist (without meaningful entries), initial diplomacy/RPG entries are auto-seeded to avoid prompt loss after upgrade.

0.6.6
- Fixed: Prompt Workbench variable panel now reuses the RimTalk variable browser (search/group/insert), so clicking a variable inserts directly into the current entry.
- Fixed: variable insertion now follows RimTalk editor behavior by inserting at cursor when the editor is focused, with a safe append fallback when focus is unavailable.
- Compatibility: legacy prompt seeding now splits combined prompt text into multiple entries by section headers (for example `[Section]` and `=== Section ===`) to improve entry completeness while keeping old saves/prompt files compatible.






- Changed: removed runtime exposure of `dialogue.diplomacy_dialogue.*` and `system.rimtalk.json_format` Scriban variables; legacy templates now auto-migrate to inline section text or the currently resolved JSON instruction text, and the old variables are blocked going forward.

0.7.23
- Refactor: introduced a strict Prompt Node channel-allowlist in `PromptUnifiedNodeSchemaCatalog` as the single source of truth for node-channel legality.
- Fixed: `PromptUnifiedCatalog` now normalizes node content and node layouts with channel constraints; illegal cross-channel nodes are removed with explicit error logs.
- Fixed: runtime `GetOrderedNodeLayouts(...)` now returns only channel-allowed nodes, preventing RPG/diplomacy/image prompt pipelines from cross-channel node injection.
- Fixed: Prompt Workbench node editing now filters by current channel; channels without nodes automatically fall back to Section mode to prevent invalid edits.
- Fixed: Workbench unified composer now builds default node layouts from channel-allowed nodes only, eliminating cross-channel node pollution in preview.

0.7.24
- Fixed: fully separated runtime assembly from workbench preview assembly. Runtime entry points (diplomacy/strategy/RPG) now force `deterministicPreview=false`, eliminating `PreviewFaction/preview_*` leakage in formal prompts.
- Refactor: upgraded prompt-domain validity from null-object checks to semantic completeness checks. Required: full diplomacy default action set, non-empty `ResponseFormat.JsonTemplate`, and non-empty key node templates (`api_limits/quest_guidance/response_contract`).
- Refactor: normalized action source to diplomacy-only. Removed diplomacy+social action merge path; social domain now keeps template text only.
- Added: `SystemPromptDomainConfig.PromptDomainSchemaVersion` (single-anchor, current=1) with one-time idempotent startup migration tracking.
- Added: startup self-heal for invalid custom prompt domains. The loader now backs up `Prompt/Custom` to `Prompt/Custom/_backup/<timestamp>/`, rebuilds from default-only source, and writes back repaired custom payload.
- Fixed: runtime fail-fast behavior. Empty critical runtime nodes or empty `ResponseFormat.JsonTemplate` now throw `PromptRenderException` and block request execution (no silent downgrade).
- Compatibility: disabling `send_image` now only marks that action as blocked and does not affect injection of other diplomacy actions.

0.7.25
- Changed: rewrote Prompt Workbench default output_specification by channel, with explicit response-format boundaries for diplomacy/proactive diplomacy/RPG/proactive RPG/social/image/summary/persona bootstrap/archive compression.
- Fixed: tightened the diplomacy_strategy default output format to JSON-only and strict strategy_output_contract compliance, disallowing mixed natural-language or markdown output.
- Synced: aligned default output-format texts across PromptSectionCatalog_Default.json, RimTalkPromptEntries_Default.json, and PromptUnifiedCatalog_Default.json to remove source drift.

0.7.37
- Added: a unified immersion guard `ImmersionOutputGuard` that validates visible dialogue only and intentionally ignores trailing `{"actions":[...]}` JSON; fail-fast blocks are triggered by parenthetical metadata, mechanic keywords, and status-panel numeric sentence patterns.
- Fixed: diplomacy parser/display chain now enforces the same guard in `AIResponseParser.NormalizeDialogueText` and `Dialog_DiplomacyDialogue.AddAIResponseToSession(...)`, preventing direct session rendering of leakage text.
- Fixed: RPG parser/display chain now enforces the same guard in `LLMRpgApiResponse.SanitizeDialogueContent` and `Dialog_RPGPawnDialogue.RequestContext.NormalizeVisibleNpcDialogueText(...)`.
- Coverage: proactive push channels now reuse the same guard in `GameComponent_NpcDialoguePushManager.SanitizeModelOutput(...)` and `GameComponent_PawnRpgDialoguePushManager.Generation.SanitizeModelOutput(...)`.
- Added: request-layer violation-aware retry in `AIChatServiceAsync.ProcessRequestCoroutine(...)`; on immersion violation, append a violation reason tag and retry once only, then return a local in-character fallback line if the second response still violates.
- Changed: hardened diplomacy/RPG response contract text and `dialogue.response_contract_body` fallback instruction with explicit immersion constraints (no parenthetical metadata, no mechanic-value leakage, no status-panel numeric phrasing).
- Changed: tightened `ImmersionOutputGuard` mechanic leakage detection from broad keyword-contains matching to context-aware regex matching, reducing false positive replacements for normal in-character dialogue.
- Changed: added a hard contract line to `dialogue.response_contract_body`: "Do not imitate meta-annotation style from history; history provides plot facts only, not output style," to suppress replay of history pollution like "(no gameplay effect)".
- Added: localized fallback keys `RimChat_ImmersionFallback_Diplomacy` and `RimChat_ImmersionFallback_Rpg` for second-failure local fallback lines.
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.7.37`.

0.7.45
- Fixed: restored non-verbal constraint injection on the RPG request path by wiring `AppendNonVerbalPromptConstraint(...)` at the end of `BuildRpgSystemPromptForRequest(...)`, so animal/baby/mechanoid targets keep a consistent `sound(thought)` contract across request and display stages.
- Changed: strengthened RPG output-format contract text (C# fallback + `Prompt/Default/PawnDialoguePrompt_Default.json`) to require visible NPC replies to stay one-line and prefer one concise sentence.
- Kept: no local hard truncation and no player-input rewriting; existing sanitization/immersion chain (`SanitizeDialogueContent` + `NormalizeVisibleNpcDialogueText`) remains the runtime enforcement path.

0.7.47
- Added: introduced a global shared cooldown pool for proactive diplomacy (Faction), fixed at 1 in-game hour (2500 ticks); when blocked, triggers are delayed via queue instead of being delivered immediately.
- Changed: critical causal warnings (`WarningThreat + Severity>=3`) no longer bypass the global shared cooldown and are now rate-limited by the same 1-hour gate.
- Changed: debug trigger `DebugForceRandomProactiveDialogue()` now routes through the normal trigger pipeline (`HandleTriggerContext`), so it follows the same global cooldown, busy checks, queueing, and reinitiate cooldown rules.

0.9.49
- Fixed: `pay_prisoner_ransom` parser dedup no longer collapses actions by `action + reason`; multiple entries with different `target_pawn_load_id` are now preserved in the same turn.
- Fixed: strict fail-fast remains in place. Duplicate ransom entries for the same target are dropped at parse stage with logs, while batch execution still blocks on duplicate/missing targets and total-offer window violations.
- Added: structured parser summary logs for ransom actions: `kept_targets`, `dropped_duplicate_targets`, and `kept_without_target`.
- Added: batch ransom validation failure logs now include explicit `expected_targets` and `actual_targets` for faster root-cause diagnosis.

0.9.63
- Root fix: tightened the `request_item_airdrop` confirmation state machine so opening the confirm dialog now invalidates stale pending-selection, async-request, and trade-card runtime state before commit, preventing regressions back into `selection_manual_choice`.
- Added: explicit airdrop runtime stages `Idle/SelectingCandidate/PreparedAwaitingConfirm/Committing/Completed/Failed/Cancelled` as the single source of truth across confirmation, commit, failure, and cancel flows.
- Improved: confirmation commit now fail-fast blocks stale pending state and logs `AirdropStalePendingBlocked` instead of letting old selection state re-enter and soft-lock the dialogue.
- Added: diagnostic logs `AirdropStateTransition`, `AirdropConfirmOpen`, `AirdropConfirmCommitStart`, `AirdropConfirmCommitResult`, and `AirdropPendingIntentInvalidated` for direct `Player.log` tracing.

0.9.71
- Root fix: added `DialogueResponseEnvelopeParser` and moved RPG / diplomacy / proactive dialogue outputs to a structured main contract with `visible_dialogue` as the primary visible field and `actions` as separate action data.
- Root fix: `AIChatServiceAsync` now performs envelope fail-fast validation on real dialogue flows before immersion, text-integrity, and action-contract checks, preventing invalid raw model text from reaching UI consumers.
- Added: `ModelOutputSanitizer.SplitVisibleAndTrailingActions` and `ComposeVisibleAndTrailingActions` as the single source of truth for visible-text and action-JSON splitting.
- Added: `ImmersionOutputGuard.ReasoningLeakage` to block unlabeled chain-of-thought, rule restatements, and analysis-style wording from leaking into visible dialogue.
- Changed: diplomacy controllers, RPG controllers, and proactive push flows now consume normalized dialogue envelopes or their canonicalized results instead of slicing raw strings ad hoc.
- Changed: thought-chain defaults are now disabled for all channels; the config and node remain only for migration compatibility and no longer act as a runtime safety boundary.
- Changed: default RPG / diplomacy prompt contracts now require the structured JSON dialogue protocol; legacy `dialogue + trailing actions JSON` remains as minimal input compatibility only.
- Docs: synchronized `About/About.xml`, `doc/Index.md`, `doc/Api.md`, `doc/config.md`, and `doc/VersionLog.txt`.

0.9.88
- Changed: diplomacy presence forced durations are now fixed values: `go_offline` = 2 hours, `set_dnd` = 4 hours. `PresenceForcedOfflineHours` is no longer used by forced-state runtime.
- Root fix: `RefreshPresenceOnDialogueOpen(...)` now restores to `Online` immediately when forced offline/DND expires, instead of re-entering schedule evaluation first.
- Compatibility: legacy saves with long forced timers are clamped on refresh to `currentTick + cap` (2h offline / 4h DND).
- UI: the `PresenceForcedOfflineHours` slider is retained, and its label now explicitly states it does not affect `go_offline/set_dnd` forced durations.
- Docs: synchronized `doc/Index.md`, `doc/Api.md`, and `doc/config.md`.

0.9.1018
- Root fix: proactive diplomacy messages and social news now use precomputed `DiplomacyPromptRuntimeSnapshot`, removing synchronous heavy dynamic scans from the request hot path.
- Added: `IDiplomacyPromptSnapshotCache` + `DiplomacyPromptSnapshotCache` with load-time frame-budget warmup, per-faction snapshot lookup, and invalidation by relation/memory/world-event/prompt-file changes.
- Changed: `PromptPersistenceService.BuildUnifiedChannelSystemPrompt(...)` now accepts optional `runtimeSnapshot`; snapshot scope reuses precomputed dynamic blocks while preserving default behavior.
- Changed: `GameComponent_NpcDialoguePushManager.StartGeneration(...)` now fail-fast defers when snapshot is not ready (short delayed requeue) instead of doing same-frame synchronous recompute.
- Changed: `SocialNewsPromptBuilder.BuildMessages(...)` and `GameComponent_DiplomacyManager.SocialCircle.NewsRequests` now share the same snapshot cache; snapshot misses enter delayed retry queue to avoid seed loss and duplicate full scans.
- Changed: `GameComponent_DiplomacyManager.GameComponentTick()` now runs snapshot warmup budget (1 build per tick) and drains deferred social-news retry items.
- Version: bumped `About/About.xml` to `0.9.1018`.
